RVV benchmark PULP Ara

These are preliminary results for PULP Ara. It is an RVV1.0 coprocessor to the OpenHW CVA6 processor.

Benchmarks were run on an FPGA using FireSim. For details about the setup refer to this repository.

After the initial tests, it seems that PULP Ara doesn't support the entire RVV1.0 instruction set and either throws "Unsupported instruction" error, or hangs the processor altogether. Because of this only instruction test has been performed with limited number of test (you can see the difference between upstream and compatible tests here).

A test is considered successful if it executes reliably in all test cases. Mind that some tests that are omitted may be partially working (e.g., `.vv` works but `.vi` doesn't or `ta` works but `tu` doesn't), or may have disfunctional setup routine.
